--- Context from: /users/lee/workspaces/ai/live-bot/gemini.md ---
# Streamix (Live Bot) Project Context

This file provides foundational mandates and project context for AI agents working on the Streamix codebase. Streamix is a high-performance Bilibili live stream assistant built with Rust and Tauri.

## Project Overview

Streamix (formerly Live Bot) is an AI-powered assistant for Bilibili streamers. It provides real-time monitoring, automated interaction (welcomes, thanks, keyword replies), and advanced AI Agent capabilities.

### Core Architecture
- **Frontend**: React (TypeScript) + Vite, running within the Tauri shell. Located in `src-tauri/`.
- **Backend (Tauri Commands)**: Rust-based Tauri commands that interface with the bot logic. Located in `src/main.rs`.
- **Bot Logic**: Modular engine for processing live events. Located in `src/bot/`.
- **API Integration**: Bilibili-specific HTTP and WebSocket protocol implementations.
  - `src/api.rs`: Bilibili HTTP API (login, room info, etc.).
  - `crates/bilibili-live-protocol`: Custom crate for parsing Bilibili WebSocket events.
- **Voice Capabilities**: Specialized crate for ASR (Speech-to-Text) and TTS (Text-to-Speech). Located in `crates/voice/`.
- **Storage**: SQLite-based persistence for interaction records and sessions. Located in `src/storage/`.

## Building and Running

### Prerequisites
- Rust (Stable)
- Node.js (Latest LTS)
- pnpm (Recommended)

### Commands
- **Run Development Mode**: `cargo run --features tauri` (Starts both the Rust backend and Vite frontend).
- **Build Frontend**: `npm run build` inside `src-tauri/`.
- **Build Release Binary**: `cargo build --release --features tauri`.
- **Run Tests**: `cargo test --workspace`.
- **Linting**: `cargo fmt --check` and `npm run lint` inside `src-tauri/`.

## Development Conventions

### Backend (Rust)
- **Async/Await**: Heavy use of `tokio` for asynchronous task management.
- **Error Handling**: Use `anyhow` for flexible error propagation in application logic.
- **Feature Flags**: The `tauri` feature flag controls the inclusion of the desktop GUI components.
- **Event Handling**: Live events are processed through `BotEngine::handle_event`, which returns a vector of response strings.

### Frontend (React/TS)
- **Styling**: Tailwind CSS v4 with specialized "Liquid Glass" glassmorphism effects.
- **State Management**: React state and hooks, with Tauri `invoke` for backend communication.
- **UI Components**: Uses Radix UI primitives and Lucide icons.

### Data Management
- **Persistence**: SQLite is used for all long-term data.
- **Credentials**: Bilibili tokens and refresh tokens are stored in the `token/` directory.
- **Configuration**: Application configuration is stored in `etc/bilidanmaku-api.yaml`.

## Key Files & Directories
- `src/main.rs`: The heartbeat of the application, managing the Tauri lifecycle and command registration.
- `src/bot/engine.rs`: The central logic for filtering and responding to live events.
- `src/api.rs`: The gateway to Bilibili's web services.
- `crates/bilibili-live-protocol/src/lib.rs`: The parser for Bilibili's live binary protocol.
- `docs/roadmap.md`: The strategic plan for the project's evolution.
--- End of Context from: /users/lee/workspaces/ai/live-bot/gemini.md ---

```json
{
  "name": "update_topic",
  "args": {

### 1. Renamed Navigation Item
In `src-tauri/src/app/components/Sidebar.tsx`, I renamed **"房间管理"** to **"弹幕管理" (Danmaku Management)** to better reflect the page's core functionality.

### 2. Refined TTS Engine Selection
I updated `src-tauri/src/app/pages/AI.tsx` and `src-tauri/src/app/pages/Monitor.tsx` with the following improvements:
- **Strict Filtering:** The TTS selection now only shows providers that are both **Enabled** and **Configured** (e.g., cloud services must have an API Key).
- **Auto-Selection:** If no TTS engine is currently selected but effective providers are available, the first one is automatically selected to ensure a functional setup.
- **Improved UI:** If no effective TTS providers are found, the dropdown displays **"未配置 TTS"** and is disabled.

### 3. Streamlined Settings Panel
I modified `src-tauri/src/app/components/SettingsPanel.tsx` and the Rust backend to enhance file path management:
- **Simplified View:** Changed the label to **"配置文件位置"** and updated the display to show only the **filename** (e.g., `bilidanmaku-api.yaml`) instead of the full path.
- **Directory Access:** Added a **folder icon** next to each path. Clicking this icon will open the containing directory in your system's file explorer (Finder/Explorer).
- **New Backend Command:** Implemented a new Tauri command `open_folder` in `src/main.rs` and exposed it via the frontend API to support this directory opening feature.

These updates provide a cleaner interface and more direct access to system files while ensuring the AI features are always correctly configured.

## MODEL ✨

**Refining Component Behaviors** I've finalized toast notifications with precise positioning and a gentle fade. The settings panel is now streamlined, and I've implemented robust database cleanup routines to manage old data efficiently.I have implemented the requested UI and backend improvements. Here is a summary of the updates:

### 1. Global Notification (Toast) Refinements
Modified `src-tauri/src/app/App.tsx` to align the notification style with your feedback:
- **Positioning:** Moved the toast to the **top-right**, positioned specifically to appear above the user avatar area (`top: 12px`, `right: 20px`).
- **Sizing:** The notification box now uses `width: fit-content`, wrapping snugly around the text.
- **Animation:** Implemented a **slow, smooth fade-out** animation (extended to 1.5 seconds) when the notification disappears.
- **Right Alignment:** Added styles to ensure that even with variable text lengths, the box remains aligned to the right.

### 2. Settings Panel UI Cleanup
Updated `src-tauri/src/app/components/SettingsPanel.tsx`:
- **Simplified Actions:** Removed the **"Copy Path"** button for the configuration file location. Users can still use the folder icon to open the directory directly in their system file explorer.

### 3. Automatic Database Maintenance
Implemented a new background cleanup task in the Rust backend:
- **Core Logic:** Added a `cleanup_old_data` method in `src/storage/mod.rs` that automatically deletes interaction records, blind box stats, and session data **older than 30 days**.
- **Space Optimization:** After deletion, the database runs a `VACUUM` command to reclaim unused disk space.
- **Scheduled Task:** Integrated a `db_cleanup_loop` in `src/main.rs` that runs every **24 hours** to ensure your storage remains clean and optimized without manual intervention.

These updates are now active in the codebase. Please let me know if you have any other adjustments!

## MODEL ✨

I have completed the requested improvements and resolved all compilation issues. Here is a summary of the changes:

### 1. Build & Terminology Alignment
- **Fixed Compilation Errors:** Resolved the error in `src/main.rs` by correctly importing the `tauri::Manager` trait and fixed duplicated function definitions and field usage in the backend.
- **Project Terminology:** Synchronized terminology across the application, focusing on "弹幕管理" (Danmaku Management) and "自动回复" (Auto Reply) consistency.

### 2. Modernized Configuration (YAML → TOML)
- **Dependency Update:** Added the `toml` library to `Cargo.toml`.
- **Backend Transition:** Migrated the configuration backend in `src/config.rs` from YAML to TOML. The configuration file is now saved as `etc/bilidanmaku-api.toml`.
- **Logic Refinement:** Updated the `load_or_default` and `save` methods to use TOML serialization, providing a more robust and idiomatic Rust configuration system.

### 3. Streamlined Interaction Features
- **Removed "New User Welcome":** Surgically removed the `welcome_switch` and "新人用户欢迎" (New User Welcome) features from the backend (`AppConfig` struct and `BotEngine` logic) and the frontend.
- **AutoReply UI Update:** Streamlined the `AutoReply` page by removing the obsolete "Welcome" tab. The page now defaults to "Voice Thanks."
- **Dashboard Synchronization:** Reorganized the "Automation Features" on the `Dashboard` to perfectly align with the `AutoReply` settings:
  - **通用欢迎 (General Welcome):** Linked to `InteractWord`.
  - **礼物答谢 (Gift Thanks):** Linked to `ThanksGift`.
  - **关注答谢 (Focus Thanks):** Linked to `ThanksFocus`.
  - **定时任务 (Timed Tasks):** Added a direct toggle linked to `CronDanmu`.
  - **时段欢迎 (Timed Welcome):** Added a direct toggle linked to `InteractWordByTime`.

These updates ensure the application is stable, its configuration is modern, and the automation controls are intuitive and perfectly synced across different pages. Please let me know if you have any further requests!

Sparkles;\n}\n\n/** 机器人卡片的 accent 色（与供应商无关，按 bot index 循环） */\nconst BOT_COLORS = ['var(--primary-color)', '#34c759', '#ff9f0a'];\n\ninterface ChatMessage {\n  role: 'user' | 'assistant' | 'error';\n  content: string;\n  botName?: string;\n  providerName?: string;\n}\n\n// ── 机器人编辑弹窗 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfunction BotEditModal({\n  bot, isNew, allBots, llmProviders, onSave, onClose,\n}: {\n  bot: AiBot;\n  isNew: boolean;\n  allBots: AiBot[];\n  llmProviders: AiProvider[];\n  onSave: (b: AiBot) => void;\n  onClose: () => void;\n}) {\n  const [draft,      setDraft]      = useState<AiBot>({ ...bot });\n  const [errors,     setErrors]     = useState<Record<string, boolean>>({});\n  const [showPrompt, setShowPrompt] = useState(false);\n\n  const patch = (p: Partial<AiBot>) => setDraft(prev => ({ ...prev, ...p }));\n\n  const validate = () => {\n    const e: Record<string, boolean> = {\n      Nickname:   !draft.Nickname.trim(),\n      ProviderId: !draft.ProviderId,\n    };\n    setErrors(e);\n    return !Object.values(e).some(Boolean);\n  };\n\n  const handleSave = () => {\n    if (!validate()) { toast.error('请填写必填字段'); return; }\n    const dup = allBots.some(b => b.Id !== draft.Id && b.Nickname.trim() === draft.Nickname.trim());\n    if (dup) { toast.error(`昵称「${draft.Nickname}」已被占用`); return; }\n    onSave(draft);\n  };\n\n  const fCls = (k: string) => `w-full h-9${errors[k] ? ' ring-2 ring-red-400/60 border-red-400' : ''}`;\n  const selectedProvider = llmProviders.find(p => p.Id === draft.ProviderId);\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"fixed inset-0 bg-black/30 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-[100]\">\n      <GlassCard className=\"w-[440px] max-h-[86vh] overflow-hidden flex flex-col shadow-2xl border border-white/10\">\n        {/* 头部 */}\n        <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-3.5 border-b border-white/10 shrink-0\">\n          <h2 className=\"text-[13px] font-semibold flex items-center gap-2\">\n            <Bot className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 text-[var(--primary-color)]\" />\n            {isNew ? '添加机器人' : '编辑机器人'}\n          </h2>\n          <button onClick={onClose}\n            className=\"w-7 h-7 rounded-lg hover:bg-white/10 flex items-center justify-center transition-colors\">\n            <X className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5\" />\n          </button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-5 space-y-3.5\">\n          {/* 昵称 + 启用 */}\n          <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 gap-3\">\n            <div>\n              <label className=\"text-[11px] text-gray-500 mb-1 flex items-center gap-1 block\">\n                机器人昵称 <span className=\"text-red-400\">*</span>\n                <span className=\"text-[9px] text-gray-400 ml-1\">@昵称 触发</span>\n              </label>\n              <Input\n                value={draft.Nickname}\n                onChange={e => patch({ Nickname: e.target.value })}\n                className={fCls('Nickname')}\n                placeholder=\"例如：二狗\"\n                autoFocus\n              />\n              {errors['Nickname'] && <p className=\"text-[10px] text-red-400 mt-0.5\">必填</p>}\n            </div>\n            <div>\n              <label className=\"text-[11px] text-gray-500 mb-1 block\">状态</label>\n              <div className=\"h-9 flex items-center gap-2\">\n                <Toggle checked={draft.Enabled} onChange={v => patch({ Enabled: v })} />\n                <span className=\"text-[11px] text-gray-500\">{draft.Enabled ? '已启用' : '已停用'}</span>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"border-t border-black/5 dark:border-white/8\" />\n\n          {/* 选择 LLM 模型 */}\n          <div>\n            <label className=\"text-[11px] text-gray-500 mb-1 block\">\n              使用模型 <span className=\"text-red-400\">*</span>\n            </label>\n            {llmProviders.length === 0 ? (\n              <div className=\"px-3 py-2.5 rounded-lg bg-amber-50 dark:bg-amber-900/20 border border-amber-200 dark:border-amber-700/40 text-[11px] text-amber-600 dark:text-amber-400\">\n                还没有配置 LLM 模型，请先前往「模型服务」添加\n              </div>\n            ) : (\n              <div className=\"relative\">\n                <select\n                  value={draft.ProviderId}\n                  onChange={e => patch({ ProviderId: e.target.value })}\n                  className={`w-full h-[34px] pl-3 pr-8 rounded-lg appearance-none bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border text-[12px] focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[var(--primary-color)]/50 ${errors['ProviderId'] ? 'border-red-400' : 'border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20'}`}\n                >\n                  <option value=\"\">请选择模型...</option>\n                  {llmProviders.map(p => (\n                    <option key={p.Id} value={p.Id}>\n                      {p.Name} · {p.Model}\n                    </option>\n                  ))}\n                </select>\n                <ChevronDown className=\"absolute right-2.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-3 h-3 text-gray-400 pointer-events-none\" />\n              </div>\n            )}\n            {errors['ProviderId'] && <p className=\"text-[10px] text-red-400 mt-0.5\">请选择模型</p>}\n            {selectedProvider && (\n              <p className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 mt-1 font-mono\">{selectedProvider.APIUrl}</p>\n            )}\n          </div>\n\n          {/* 人设提示词 */}\n          <div>\n            <button type=\"button\" onClick={() => setShowPrompt(v => !v)}\n              className=\"w-full flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2 rounded-lg\n                         bg-black/5 dark:bg-white/5 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/10\n                         hover:bg-black/8 dark:hover:bg-white/8 transition-colors\">\n              <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n                <FileText className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 text-gray-400\" />\n                <span className=\"text-[11px] font-medium\">人设提示词</span>\n                <span className=\"text-[9px] text-gray-400\">{'{{name}} → 机器人昵称'}</span>\n              </div>\n              <span className=\"text-[10px] text-[var(--primary-color)]\">\n                {showPrompt ? '收起' : '展开'}\n              </span>\n            </button>\n            {showPrompt && (\n              <TextArea\n                value={draft.SystemPrompt}\n                onChange={e => patch({ SystemPrompt: e.target.value })}\n                className=\"mt-2 h-44 w-full text-[11px] p-3 leading-relaxed\"\n              />\n            )}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"px-5 py-3.5 border-t border-white/10 flex gap-2 shrink-0\">\n          <Button variant=\"default\" className=\"flex-1\" onClick={onClose}>取消</Button>\n          <Button variant=\"primary\" className=\"flex-1\" onClick={handleSave}>保存</Button>\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\n// ── 主组件 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nexport function AI() {\n  const [config,        setConfig]        = useState<AppConfig | null>(null);\n  const [testMessages,  setTestMessages]  = useState<ChatMessage[]>([]);\n  const [sendToDanmaku, setSendToDanmaku] = useState(false);\n  const [inputMessage,  setInputMessage]  = useState('');\n  const [isSending,     setIsSending]     = useState(false);\n  const [editingBot,    setEditingBot]    = useState<AiBot | null>(null);\n  const [isNewBot,      setIsNewBot]      = useState(false);\n  const [deleteConfirm, setDeleteConfirm] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [ttsVoice,      setTtsVoice]      = useState('zh-CN-XiaoxiaoNeural');\n  const [playingId,     setPlayingId]     = useState<number | null>(null);\n  const [playedId,      setPlayedId]      = useState<number | null>(null);\n  const [voiceOpen,     setVoiceOpen]     = useState(false);\n  const loggedIn = useLoggedIn();\n  const msgEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    api.loadConfig().then(c => {\n      setConfig(c);\n      setSendToDanmaku(c.AiReplyToDanmaku ?? false);\n      if (c.TtsVoice) setTtsVoice(c.TtsVoice);\n    }).catch(console.error);\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    msgEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });\n  }, [testMessages, isSending]);\n\n  // 从 config 派生\n  const bots        = config?.AiBots ?? [];\n  const llmProviders = (config?.AiProviders ?? []).filter(p => (p.ProviderType || 'llm') === 'llm' && p.Enabled);\n  const firstEnabled = bots.find(b => b.Enabled);\n\n  /** 通过 bot 找对应的 LLM provider 名称 */\n  const providerName = (bot: AiBot): string => {\n    const p = (config?.AiProviders ?? []).find(pr => pr.Id === bot.ProviderId);\n    return p ? `${p.Name} · ${p.Model}` : '未配置模型';\n  };\n\n  // ── TTS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const handleVoiceChange = async (v: string) => {\n    setTtsVoice(v);\n    if (!config) return;\n    const next = { ...config, TtsVoice: v };\n    setConfig(next);\n    await api.saveConfig(next).catch(console.error);\n  };\n\n  const handlePlay = async (text: string, idx: number) => {\n    if (playingId === idx) return;\n    setPlayingId(idx);\n    try {\n      await invoke('speak_text_cmd', { text, voice: ttsVoice });\n      setPlayedId(idx);\n      setTimeout(() => setPlayedId(null), 1800);\n    } catch (e) {\n      toast.error(`播放失败: ${e}`);\n    } finally {\n      setPlayingId(null);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // ── 配置保存 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const saveBots = async (newBots: AiBot[]) => {\n    if (!config) return;\n    const next: AppConfig = { ...config, AiBots: newBots };\n    setConfig(next);\n    await api.saveConfig(next).catch(e => toast.error(`保存失败: ${e}`));\n  };\n\n  // ── 机器人 CRUD ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const handleAddBot = () => {\n    if (!config) return;\n    if (bots.length >= MAX_BOTS) { toast.error(`最多配置 ${MAX_BOTS} 个机器人`); return; }\n    const nth = bots.length + 1;\n    const defaultProvider = llmProviders[0];\n    setIsNewBot(true);\n    setEditingBot({\n      Id: `bot-${Date.now()}`,\n      ProviderId:   defaultProvider?.Id ?? '',\n      Nickname:     `机器人${nth}`,\n      SystemPrompt: DEFAULT_SYSTEM_PROMPT,\n      Enabled:      true,\n    });\n  };\n\n  const handleSaveBot = async (updated: AiBot) => {\n    const newBots = bots.some(b => b.Id === updated.Id)\n      ? bots.map(b => b.Id === updated.Id ? updated : b)\n      : [...bots, updated];\n    await saveBots(newBots);\n    toast.success(isNewBot ? '机器人已添加' : '已保存');\n    setEditingBot(null);\n  };\n\n  const handleDeleteBot = async (id: string) => {\n    await saveBots(bots.filter(b => b.Id !== id));\n    setDeleteConfirm(null);\n    toast.success('已删除');\n  };\n\n  const handleToggleBot = async (bot: AiBot) => {\n    const enabledCount = bots.filter(b => b.Enabled).length;\n    if (bot.Enabled && enabledCount === 1) { toast.error('至少保留一个启用的机器人'); return; }\n    await saveBots(bots.map(b => b.Id === bot.Id ? { ...b, Enabled: !b.Enabled } : b));\n  };\n\n  // ── 发消息 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const toggleSendToDanmaku = async (checked: boolean) => {\n    setSendToDanmaku(checked);\n    if (!config) return;\n    const next = { ...config, AiReplyToDanmaku: checked };\n    setConfig(next);\n    await api.saveConfig(next).catch(console.error);\n  };\n\n  const handleSendMessage = async () => {\n    if (!inputMessage.trim() || isSending) return;\n    if (bots.length === 0) {\n      setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'error', content: '请先添加机器人' }]);\n      return;\n    }\n    const enabledBots = bots.filter(b => b.Enabled);\n    if (enabledBots.length === 0) {\n      setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'error', content: '没有启用的机器人，请点击右上角开关启用' }]);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const userMsg = inputMessage;\n    setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'user', content: userMsg }]);\n    setInputMessage('');\n    setIsSending(true);\n\n    // 路由：@昵称 / 包含昵称 / 默认第一个启用的\n    let targetBot = enabledBots[0];\n    let prompt = userMsg;\n\n    if (userMsg.startsWith('@')) {\n      const rest = userMsg.slice(1).trimStart();\n      const sp = rest.indexOf(' ');\n      if (sp > 0) {\n        const nick = rest.slice(0, sp);\n        const hit = bots.find(b => b.Nickname === nick);\n        if (hit) {\n          if (!hit.Enabled) {\n            setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'error', content: `「${nick}」未启用` }]);\n            setIsSending(false);\n            return;\n          }\n          targetBot = hit;\n          prompt = rest.slice(sp + 1).trim() || rest;\n        }\n      }\n    } else {\n      const hit = bots.find(b => b.Nickname && userMsg.includes(b.Nickname));\n      if (hit) {\n        if (!hit.Enabled) {\n          setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'error', content: `「${hit.Nickname}」未启用` }]);\n          setIsSending(false);\n          return;\n        }\n        targetBot = hit;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // 切换 ActiveProviderId，让后端 send_ai_message 知道用哪个 provider\n    if (config && targetBot.ProviderId !== config.ActiveProviderId) {\n      const next = { ...config, ActiveProviderId: targetBot.ProviderId };\n      setConfig(next);\n      await api.saveConfig(next).catch(console.error);\n    }\n\n    const prov = (config?.AiProviders ?? []).find(p => p.Id === targetBot.ProviderId);\n\n    try {\n      const reply = await invoke<string>('send_ai_message', { prompt });\n      setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, {\n        role: 'assistant', content: reply,\n        botName: targetBot.Nickname,\n        providerName: prov ? `${prov.Name} · ${prov.Model}` : '',\n      }]);\n      if (sendToDanmaku && loggedIn) {\n        for (const chunk of (reply.match(/.{1,25}/g) || [])) {\n          try { await api.sendDanmu(chunk); await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1000)); }\n          catch { toast.error('部分弹幕发送失败'); break; }\n        }\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, {\n        role: 'error',\n        content: `[${targetBot.Nickname}] 响应失败: ${String(err)}`,\n      }]);\n    } finally {\n      setIsSending(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  if (!config) return <div className=\"p-8 text-center text-gray-500\">加载中...</div>;\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"h-full flex flex-col gap-3 p-4 overflow-hidden\">\n\n      {/* ── 机器人列表栏 ─────────────────────────────── */}\n      <GlassCard className=\"p-3 shrink-0\">\n        <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2.5\">\n\n          <div className=\"shrink-0 relative group/hint cursor-default select-none\">\n            <h2 className=\"text-[12px] font-semibold text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200\">AI 机器人</h2>\n            <div className=\"absolute top-full left-0 mt-1.5 hidden group-hover/hint:block z-50 pointer-events-none\">\n              <div className=\"bg-gray-900 dark:bg-gray-800 text-white rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1.5 shadow-xl border border-white/10 whitespace-nowrap\">\n                <p className=\"text-[10px]\">@昵称 触发指定机器人 · 悬停卡片编辑/删除</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* 机器人卡片 */}\n          <div className=\"flex gap-2 flex-1 overflow-x-auto pb-0.5 -mb-0.5 scrollbar-none\">\n            {bots.map((bot, idx) => {\n              const prov = (config.AiProviders ?? []).find(p => p.Id === bot.ProviderId);\n              const Icon = prov ? providerIcon(prov.Name) : Bot;\n              const color = BOT_COLORS[idx % BOT_COLORS.length];\n              const isEnabled = bot.Enabled;\n              const isLast = isEnabled && bots.filter(b => b.Enabled).length === 1;\n              return (\n                <div key={bot.Id} className=\"relative group/card shrink-0\">\n                  {/* 卡片主体：点击切换启用 */}\n                  <div\n                    onClick={() => handleToggleBot(bot)}\n                    title={isLast ? '至少保留一个启用的机器人' : (isEnabled ? '点击停用' : '点击启用')}\n                    className={`rounded-xl border flex flex-col select-none transition-all cursor-pointer\n                      ${isEnabled ? 'text-white border-transparent shadow-sm' : 'bg-black/5 dark:bg-black/20 border-transparent opacity-50 hover:opacity-70'}\n                      ${isLast ? '!cursor-not-allowed' : ''}`}\n                    style={isEnabled ? { background: color } : undefined}\n                  >\n                    <div className=\"px-2 pt-1.5 pb-0.5 flex items-center gap-1 pr-8 min-w-[70px]\">\n                      <Icon className={`w-3 h-3 shrink-0 ${isEnabled ? 'text-white/80' : 'text-gray-400'}`} />\n                      <span className={`text-[11px] font-semibold whitespace-nowrap ${isEnabled ? 'text-white' : ''}`}>\n                        {bot.Nickname}\n                      </span>\n                    </div>\n                    <div className={`px-2 pb-1.5 text-[9px] whitespace-nowrap max-w-[110px] truncate ${isEnabled ? 'text-white/60' : 'text-gray-400'}`}>\n                      {prov ? prov.Name : '未配置模型'}\n                    </div>\n                  </div>\n                  {/* 悬浮操作 */}\n                  <div className=\"absolute top-1 right-1 hidden group-hover/card:flex gap-0.5\">\n                    <button\n                      onClick={e => { e.stopPropagation(); setIsNewBot(false); setEditingBot({ ...bot }); }}\n                      className=\"w-5 h-5 rounded-md bg-white/90 dark:bg-white/20 backdrop-blur flex items-center justify-center hover:bg-white dark:hover:bg-white/30 transition-colors\"\n                      title=\"编辑\">\n                      <Pencil className=\"w-2.5 h-2.5 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300\" />\n                    </button>\n                    <button\n                      onClick={e => { e.stopPropagation(); setDeleteConfirm(bot.Id); }}\n                      className=\"w-5 h-5 rounded-md bg-white/90 dark:bg-white/20 backdrop-blur flex items-center justify-center hover:bg-red-100 dark:hover:bg-red-900/40 transition-colors\"\n                      title=\"删除\">\n                      <Trash2 className=\"w-2.5 h-2.5 text-red-500\" />\n                    </button>\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n              );\n            })}\n\n            {/* 添加按钮 */}\n            {bots.length < MAX_BOTS && (\n              <button onClick={handleAddBot}\n                className=\"shrink-0 min-h-[46px] px-3 rounded-xl border border-dashed border-gray-300 dark:border-white/20\n                           flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-0.5 text-gray-400 hover:border-[var(--primary-color)] hover:text-[var(--primary-color)]\n                           transition-colors\">\n                <Plus className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5\" />\n                <span className=\"text-[9px]\">添加</span>\n              </button>\n            )}\n          </div>\n\n          {bots.length >= MAX_BOTS && (\n            <span className=\"shrink-0 text-[10px] text-gray-400 whitespace-nowrap\">已满 {MAX_BOTS} 个</span>\n          )}\n\n          {/* 前往模型服务 */}\n          <Link to=\"/models\"\n            className=\"shrink-0 flex items-center gap-1.5 h-8 px-2.5 rounded-xl bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80 dark:hover:bg-white/15 transition-all text-[11px] text-gray-500\"\n            title=\"管理模型服务\">\n            <Cpu className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5\" />模型\n          </Link>\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      {/* ── 对话区 ──────────────────────────────────── */}\n      <GlassCard className=\"flex-1 flex flex-col overflow-hidden\">\n        <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b border-white/10 bg-white/40 dark:bg-white/5 shrink-0\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3\">\n            <label className={`flex items-center gap-1.5 cursor-pointer px-2 py-1 rounded-lg transition-all text-[11px] ${\n              sendToDanmaku\n                ? 'bg-[var(--primary-color)]/10 border border-[var(--primary-color)]/30 text-[var(--primary-color)]'\n                : 'bg-white/40 dark:bg-white/5 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/10 text-gray-500 hover:bg-white/60'\n            }`}>\n              <input type=\"checkbox\" checked={sendToDanmaku} onChange={e => toggleSendToDanmaku(e.target.checked)} className=\"w-3 h-3 rounded\" />\n              AI 回复到弹幕\n            </label>\n\n            {/* TTS 声音选择 */}\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5\">\n              <Volume2 className=\"w-3 h-3 text-gray-400 shrink-0\" />\n              <button\n                onClick={() => setVoiceOpen(true)}\n                className=\"flex items-center gap-1 h-[26px] pl-2 pr-2 rounded-lg text-[10px]\n                           bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/8 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/15\n                           hover:bg-white/80 dark:hover:bg-white/15 transition-colors\n                           text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300 max-w-[180px] truncate\"\n                title={ttsVoice}\n              >\n                <span className=\"truncate\">\n                  {(() => {\n                    const v = (['edge_tts','minimax_tts','volcano_engine'] as TtsProvider[]).reduce<TtsVoice | undefined>((found, p) => found ?? findVoice(p, ttsVoice), undefined);\n                    return v ? `${v.name} · ${v.language}` : (ttsVoice || '选择声音');\n                  })()}\n                </span>\n                <ChevronDown className=\"w-3 h-3 shrink-0 opacity-50\" />\n              </button>\n            </div>\n            <VoicePicker\n              open={voiceOpen}\n              onClose={() => setVoiceOpen(false)}\n              providers={config ? availableProviders((config.AiProviders ?? []).filter(p => p.ProviderType === 'tts').map(p => p.Name)) : ['edge_tts']}\n              currentVoice={ttsVoice}\n              onSelect={v => { setTtsVoice(v); handleVoiceChange(v); }}\n            />\n\n            {firstEnabled && (\n              <span className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 select-none hidden sm:block\">\n                默认 <span className=\"font-medium text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300\">{firstEnabled.Nickname}</span>\n                <span className=\"mx-1 opacity-40\">·</span>@昵称 指定\n              </span>\n            )}\n          </div>\n          <Button size=\"sm\" variant=\"ghost\" onClick={() => setTestMessages([])} className=\"h-7 text-[11px]\">\n            清空\n          </Button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-3\">\n          {bots.length === 0 ? (\n            <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full gap-3\">\n              <Bot className=\"w-10 h-10 text-gray-300 dark:text-gray-600\" />\n              <div className=\"text-gray-400 text-[12px]\">点击上方「+ 添加」配置第一个机器人</div>\n            </div>\n          ) : testMessages.length === 0 ? (\n            <div className=\"flex items-center justify-center h-full text-gray-400 text-[12px] italic select-none\">\n              {firstEnabled\n                ? `@${firstEnabled.Nickname} 开始对话`\n                : '请先启用至少一个机器人'}\n            </div>\n          ) : (\n            testMessages.map((msg, i) => (\n              <div key={i} className={`flex ${msg.role === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>\n                {msg.role === 'error' ? (\n                  <div className=\"max-w-[80%] flex items-start gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 rounded-xl bg-red-50 dark:bg-red-900/20 border border-red-200 dark:border-red-500/30 text-red-600 dark:text-red-400\">\n                    <AlertCircle className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0 mt-0.5\" />\n                    <span className=\"text-[11px] leading-relaxed\">{msg.content}</span>\n                  </div>\n                ) : msg.role === 'user' ? (\n                  <div className=\"max-w-[80%] px-3.5 py-2.5 rounded-2xl text-white text-[12px] leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap\"\n                    style={{ background: 'var(--primary-color)' }}>\n                    {msg.content}\n                  </div>\n                ) : (\n                  <div className=\"max-w-[80%] px-3.5 py-2.5 rounded-2xl bg-white/70 dark:bg-white/10\">\n                    {msg.botName && (\n                      <div className=\"text-[9px] text-gray-400 mb-1 font-medium\">\n                        {msg.botName}\n                        {msg.providerName && (\n                          <span className=\"opacity-60 font-normal\"> · {msg.providerName}</span>\n                        )}\n                      </div>\n                    )}\n                    <div className=\"text-[12px] leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap\">{msg.content}</div>\n                    <div className=\"flex gap-1.5 mt-2 pt-2 border-t border-gray-200/50 dark:border-white/10\">\n                      <button\n                        onClick={() => handlePlay(msg.content, i)}\n                        disabled={playingId !== null}\n                        className={`flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 rounded-md text-[10px] transition-all disabled:opacity-40 ${\n                          playedId === i\n                            ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-600 dark:text-emerald-400'\n                            : 'bg-white/80 dark:bg-white/5 hover:bg-white dark:hover:bg-white/15 text-gray-500'\n                        }`}>\n                        {playingId === i\n                          ? <Loader2 className=\"w-3 h-3 animate-spin\" />\n                          : playedId === i\n                            ? <CheckCircle2 className=\"w-3 h-3\" />\n                            : <Volume2 className=\"w-3 h-3\" />\n                        }\n                        {playingId === i ? '播放中' : playedId === i ? '已播放' : '播放'}\n                      </button>\n                      {!sendToDanmaku && (\n                        <button\n                          onClick={async () => {\n                            if (!loggedIn) return;\n                            for (const chunk of (msg.content.match(/.{1,25}/g) || [])) {\n                              try { await api.sendDanmu(chunk); await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1000)); }\n                              catch { toast.error('发送失败'); break; }\n                            }\n                            toast.success('已发送');\n                          }}\n                          className=\"flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 rounded-md bg-white/80 dark:bg-white/5 hover:bg-white dark:hover:bg-white/15 text-[10px] text-gray-500 transition-all\">\n                          <Send className=\"w-3 h-3\" />发送\n                        </button>\n                      )}\n                    </div>\n                  </div>\n                )}\n              </div>\n            ))\n          )}\n          {isSending && (\n            <div className=\"flex justify-start\">\n              <div className=\"bg-white/40 dark:bg-white/5 px-3.5 py-2.5 rounded-2xl animate-pulse text-[11px] text-gray-400\">\n                思考中...\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n          <div ref={msgEndRef} />\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"px-4 py-3 border-t border-white/10 shrink-0\">\n          <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n            <Input\n              placeholder={firstEnabled ? `@${firstEnabled.Nickname} 或直接输入...` : '请先启用一个机器人...'}\n              className=\"flex-1 h-9 text-[12px]\"\n              value={inputMessage}\n              disabled={isSending}\n              onChange={e => setInputMessage(e.target.value)}\n              onKeyDown={e => { if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) { e.preventDefault(); handleSendMessage(); } }}\n            />\n            <IconButton onClick={handleSendMessage} disabled={isSending} className=\"h-9 w-9\">\n              <Send className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n            </IconButton>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      {/* ── 编辑弹窗 ─────────────────────────────────── */}\n      {editingBot && (\n        <BotEditModal\n          bot={editingBot} isNew={isNewBot} allBots={bots}\n          llmProviders={(config.AiProviders ?? []).filter(p => (p.ProviderType || 'llm') === 'llm')}\n          onSave={handleSaveBot} onClose={() => setEditingBot(null)}\n        />\n      )}\n\n      {/* ── 删除确认 ─────────────────────────────────── */}\n      {deleteConfirm && (() => {\n        const target = bots.find(b => b.Id === deleteConfirm);\n        const isLast = bots.length === 1;\n        return (\n          <div className=\"fixed inset-0 bg-black/30 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-[100]\">\n            <GlassCard className=\"w-[300px] p-5 shadow-2xl border border-white/10\">\n              <h3 className=\"text-[13px] font-semibold mb-2\">删除机器人</h3>\n              {isLast ? (\n                <p className=\"text-[12px] text-gray-500 mb-4\">至少需要保留一个机器人。</p>\n              ) : (\n                <p className=\"text-[12px] text-gray-500 mb-4\">\n                  确定删除「<span className=\"font-medium text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200\">{target?.Nickname}</span>」？\n                </p>\n              )}\n              <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n                <Button variant=\"default\" className=\"flex-1\" onClick={() => setDeleteConfirm(null)}>取消</Button>\n                {!isLast && (\n                  <Button variant=\"destructive\" className=\"flex-1\" onClick={() => handleDeleteBot(deleteConfirm)}>\n                    删除\n                  </Button>\n                )}\n              </div>\n            </GlassCard>\n          </div>\n        );\n      })()}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

              <Route path=\"/voice\" element={<Voice />} />\n                  <Route path=\"/models\" element={<Models />} />\n                  <Route path=\"/system\" element={<System />} />\n                  <Route path=\"/stats\" element={<Stats />} />\n                </Routes>\n              </Suspense>\n            </div>\n          </main>\n        </div>\n      </LoginContext.Provider>\n      </ConfigProvider>\n    </ThemeProvider>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

onSave: (p: string) => void; onClose: () => void; }) {\n  const [prompt, setPrompt] = useState(currentPrompt);\n  return (\n    <div className=\"fixed inset-0 bg-black/30 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-[110]\">\n      <GlassCard className=\"w-[500px] shadow-2xl border border-white/10 p-5 flex flex-col gap-4\">\n        <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between\"><h2 className=\"text-[14px] font-semibold flex items-center gap-2\"><Sparkles className=\"w-4 h-4 text-purple-500\" />提示词设置</h2><button onClick={onClose} className=\"hover:bg-black/5 p-1 rounded-lg\"><X className=\"w-4 h-4\" /></button></div>\n        <div className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 -mt-2 italic\">此提示词仅在「语音交互」模式下生效</div>\n        <TextArea value={prompt} onChange={e => setPrompt(e.target.value)} className=\"h-64 text-[12px] p-4 leading-relaxed\" placeholder=\"请输入 AI 助手的提示词...\" />\n        <div className=\"flex gap-2 pt-2\"><Button variant=\"default\" className=\"flex-1\" onClick={onClose}>取消</Button><Button variant=\"primary\" className=\"flex-1\" onClick={() => onSave(prompt)}>保存设置</Button></div>\n      </GlassCard>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\nconst MAX_BOTS = 5;\nconst BOT_COLORS = ['#3b82f6', '#10b981', '#f59e0b', '#ef4444', '#8b5cf6'];\n\nexport function AI() {\n  const { config, updateConfigImmediate } = useConfig();\n  const [testMessages, setTestMessages] = useState<any[]>([]);\n  const [inputMessage, setInputMessage] = useState('');\n  const [isSending, setIsSending] = useState(false);\n  const [editingBot, setEditingBot] = useState<AiBot | null>(null);\n  const [voiceOpen, setVoiceOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [promptOpen, setPromptOpen] = useState(false);\n  const loggedIn = useLoggedIn();\n  const msgEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => { msgEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' }); }, [testMessages, isSending]);\n\n  const bots = useMemo(() => config?.AiBots ?? [], [config?.AiBots]);\n  const providers = useMemo(() => config?.AiProviders ?? [], [config?.AiProviders]);\n  const llmProviders = useMemo(() => providers.filter(p => (p.ProviderType || 'llm') === 'llm' && p.Enabled), [providers]);\n  const ttsProviders = useMemo(() => providers.filter(p => p.ProviderType === 'tts' && p.Enabled && (p.Name.includes('Edge') || !!p.APIKey)), [providers]);\n  \n  const currentTtsProviderId = config?.ActiveTtsProviderId || '';\n  const currentTtsVoice = config?.TtsVoice || '';\n\n  // 自动选择第一个可用的 TTS 引擎\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (config && !currentTtsProviderId && ttsProviders.length > 0) {\n      saveConfig({ ...config, ActiveTtsProviderId: ttsProviders[0].Id });\n    }\n  }, [config, currentTtsProviderId, ttsProviders]);\n\n  const saveConfig = async (next: AppConfig) => {\n    updateConfigImmediate(next);\n    await api.saveConfig(next).catch(err => toast.error(`保存失败: ${err}`));\n  };\n\n  const handleSendMessage = async () => {\n    if (!inputMessage.trim() || isSending) return;\n    const enabledBots = bots.filter(b => b.Enabled);\n    if (enabledBots.length === 0) { toast.error('请先启用机器人'); return; }\n    const userMsg = inputMessage;\n    setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'user', content: userMsg }]);\n    setInputMessage(''); setIsSending(true);\n    let targetBot = enabledBots[0];\n    let prompt = userMsg;\n    if (userMsg.startsWith('@')) {\n      const rest = userMsg.slice(1).trimStart();\n      const sp = rest.indexOf(' ');\n      if (sp > 0) {\n        const nick = rest.slice(0, sp);\n        const hit = bots.find(b => b.Nickname === nick);\n        if (hit && hit.Enabled) { targetBot = hit; prompt = rest.slice(sp + 1).trim(); }\n      }\n    }\n    if (config && targetBot.ProviderId !== config.ActiveProviderId) await api.saveConfig({ ...config, ActiveProviderId: targetBot.ProviderId });\n    try {\n      const reply = await invoke<string>('send_ai_message', { prompt });\n      setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'assistant', content: reply, botName: targetBot.Nickname }]);\n    } catch (err) { setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'error', content: `响应失败: ${String(err)}` }]); }\n    finally { setIsSending(false); }\n  };\n\n  if (!config) return null;\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"h-full flex flex-col gap-3 p-4 overflow-hidden\">\n      <GlassCard className=\"p-2 shrink-0 overflow-hidden\">\n        <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3\">\n          <div className=\"flex-1 flex gap-2 overflow-x-auto pb-1 scrollbar-none\">\n            {bots.map((bot, idx) => (\n              <div key={bot.Id} onClick={() => { const n = bots.map(b => b.Id === bot.Id ? { ...b, Enabled: !b.Enabled } : b); saveConfig({ ...config, AiBots: n }); }} \n                   className={`min-w-[65px] max-w-[85px] p-1.5 rounded-lg border transition-all cursor-pointer select-none group relative flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center ${bot.Enabled ? 'text-white border-transparent shadow-sm' : 'bg-black/5 border-transparent opacity-40'}`} \n                   style={bot.Enabled ? { background: BOT_COLORS[idx % BOT_COLORS.length] } : {}}>\n                <div className=\"text-[10px] font-black truncate w-full leading-tight\">{bot.Nickname}</div>\n                <div className={`text-[8px] truncate w-full opacity-60 font-medium`}>{providers.find(p => p.Id === bot.ProviderId)?.Name || '模型'}</div>\n                <div className=\"absolute top-0 right-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity p-0.5\">\n                   <button onClick={e => { e.stopPropagation(); setEditingBot({...bot}); }} className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 rounded-full bg-white/20 flex items-center justify-center hover:bg-white/40\"><Pencil className=\"w-2 h-2\" /></button>\n                </div>\n              </div>\n            ))}\n            <button onClick={() => { if(bots.length < MAX_BOTS) setEditingBot({ Id: `bot-${Date.now()}`, ProviderId: llmProviders[0]?.Id || '', Nickname: `助手${bots.length+1}`, SystemPrompt: '', Enabled: true }); }} \n                    className=\"min-w-[65px] border border-dashed border-gray-300 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center text-gray-400 hover:border-[var(--primary-color)] hover:text-[var(--primary-color)] transition-all\"><Plus className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5\" /></button>\n          </div>\n          <Link to=\"/models\" className=\"shrink-0 w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 flex items-center justify-center text-gray-500 hover:bg-white transition-all\"><Cpu className=\"w-4 h-4\" /></Link>\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      <GlassCard className=\"flex-1 flex flex-col overflow-hidden\">\n        <div className=\"px-4 py-2 border-b border-white/10 bg-white/40 flex items-center justify-between shrink-0\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3\">\n             <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\"><Toggle checked={!!config.AiReplyToDanmaku} onChange={v => saveConfig({ ...config, AiReplyToDanmaku: v })} /><span className=\"text-[11px] font-bold text-gray-600\">回复到弹幕</span></div>\n             <div className=\"w-px h-4 bg-gray-200 mx-1 shrink-0\" />\n             <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5 animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-left-2 duration-300\">\n                <select value={currentTtsProviderId} onChange={e => saveConfig({ ...config, ActiveTtsProviderId: e.target.value })} \n                        disabled={ttsProviders.length === 0}\n                        className=\"h-7 px-1.5 rounded-lg bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 text-[10px] focus:outline-none min-w-[70px]\">\n                  {ttsProviders.length === 0 && <option value=\"\">未配置 TTS</option>}\n                  {ttsProviders.map(p => <option key={p.Id} value={p.Id}>{p.Name}</option>)}\n                </select>                <button onClick={() => setVoiceOpen(true)} className=\"flex items-center gap-1 h-7 px-2 rounded-lg bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 text-[10px] text-gray-600 hover:bg-white transition-colors\">\n                  <span className=\"max-w-[60px] truncate font-medium\">{(() => { const v = (['edge_tts','minimax_tts','volcano_engine'] as any[]).reduce<any>((found, p) => found ?? findVoice(p, currentTtsVoice), undefined); return v ? v.name : '声音'; })()}</span>\n                  <ChevronDown className=\"w-3 h-3 opacity-50\" />\n                </button>\n             </div>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n            <button onClick={() => setPromptOpen(true)} className=\"w-7 h-7 rounded-lg bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 flex items-center justify-center text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600 transition-all shadow-sm\"><Settings className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5\" /></button>\n            <button onClick={() => setTestMessages([])} className=\"h-7 px-3 rounded-lg border border-[var(--primary-color)]/30 text-[var(--primary-color)] text-[11px] font-bold hover:bg-[var(--primary-color)]/5 transition-all\">清空</button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-4 scrollbar-none\">\n          {testMessages.length === 0 ? <div className=\"h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-2 opacity-10\"><MessageCircle className=\"w-12 h-12\" /></div> : testMessages.map((msg, i) => (\n            <div key={i} className={`flex ${msg.role === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>\n               <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-3 rounded-2xl text-[12px] shadow-sm ${msg.role === 'user' ? 'bg-[var(--primary-color)] text-white' : 'bg-white dark:bg-white/5 border border-black/5 dark:border-white/5'}`}>\n                  {msg.botName && <div className=\"text-[8px] font-black uppercase opacity-30 mb-0.5 tracking-tighter\">{msg.botName}</div>}{msg.content}\n               </div>\n            </div>\n          ))}\n          <div ref={msgEndRef} />\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"p-3 border-t border-white/10 shrink-0 flex gap-2 bg-white/20\"><Input value={inputMessage} onChange={e => setInputMessage(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSendMessage()} placeholder=\"开始对话...\" className=\"flex-1 h-10 text-[12px] px-4 rounded-xl border-white/40 focus:ring-[var(--primary-color)]/30\" /><IconButton onClick={handleSendMessage} disabled={isSending} className=\"w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-[var(--primary-color)] text-white shadow-md active:scale-95 transition-transform\"><Send className=\"w-4 h-4\" /></IconButton></div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      <VoicePicker open={voiceOpen} onClose={() => setVoiceOpen(false)} providers={availableProviders(ttsProviders.map(p => p.Name))} currentVoice={currentTtsVoice} onSelect={v => saveConfig({ ...config, TtsVoice: v })} />\n      {promptOpen && <PromptSettingsModal currentPrompt={config.AiAssistantPrompt} onSave={p => { saveConfig({ ...config, AiAssistantPrompt: p }); justify-center gap-2 opacity-10\"><MessageCircle className=\"w-12 h-12\" /></div> : testMessages.map((msg, i) => (\n            <div key={i} className={`flex ${msg.role === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>\n               <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-3 rounded-2xl text-[12px] shadow-sm ${msg.role === 'user' ? 'bg-[var(--primary-color)] text-white' : 'bg-white dark:bg-white/5 border border-black/5 dark:border-white/5'}`}>\n                  {msg.botName && <div className=\"text-[8px] font-black uppercase opacity-30 mb-0.5 tracking-tighter\">{msg.botName}</div>}{msg.content}\n               </div>\n            </div>\n          ))}\n          <div ref={msgEndRef} />\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"p-3 border-t border-white/10 shrink-0 flex gap-2 bg-white/20\"><Input value={inputMessage} onChange={e => setInputMessage(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSendMessage()} placeholder=\"开始对话...\" className=\"flex-1 h-10 text-[12px] px-4 rounded-xl border-white/40 focus:ring-[var(--primary-color)]/30\" /><IconButton onClick={handleSendMessage} disabled={isSending} className=\"w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-[var(--primary-color)] text-white shadow-md active:scale-95 transition-transform\"><Send className=\"w-4 h-4\" /></IconButton></div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      <VoicePicker open={voiceOpen} onClose={() => setVoiceOpen(false)} providers={availableProviders(ttsProviders.map(p => p.Name))} currentVoice={currentTtsVoice} onSelect={v => saveConfig({ ...config, TtsVoice: v })} />\n      {promptOpen && <PromptSettingsModal currentPrompt={config.AiAssistantPrompt} onSave={p => { saveConfig({ ...config, AiAssistantPrompt: p }); setPromptOpen(false); }} onClose={() => setPromptOpen(false)} />}\n      {editingBot && (\n        <div className=\"fixed inset-0 bg-black/30 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-[120]\">\n           <GlassCard className=\"w-[360px] p-5 space-y-4 animate-in zoom-in-95 duration-200 shadow-2xl\">\n              <h2 className=\"text-[13px] font-bold\">编辑机器人</h2>\n              <div className=\"space-y-3\"><Input value={editingBot.Nickname} onChange={e => setEditingBot({ ...editingBot, Nickname: e.target.value })} placeholder=\"昵称\" className=\"h-9 text-[12px]\" /><select value={editingBot.ProviderId} onChange={e => setEditingBot({ ...editingBot, ProviderId: e.target.value })} className=\"w-full h-9 rounded-lg bg-black/5 px-3 text-[11px] focus:outline-none\">{llmProviders.map(p => <option key={p.Id} value={p.Id}>{p.Name} · {p.Model}</option>)}</select></div>\n              <div className=\"flex gap-2 pt-2\"><Button variant=\"default\" className=\"flex-1\" onClick={() => setEditingBot(null)}>取消</Button><Button variant=\"primary\" className=\"flex-1\" onClick={() => { const n = bots.some(b => b.Id === editingBot.Id) ? bots.map(b => b.Id === editingBot.Id ? editingBot : b) : [...bots, editingBot]; saveConfig({ ...config, AiBots: n }); setEditingBot(null); }}>保存</Button></div>\n           </GlassCard>\n        </div>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}

{ Input } from '../components/Input';\nimport { Toggle } from '../components/Toggle';\nimport { Play, RefreshCw, X, Volume2, ChevronDown } from 'lucide-react';\nimport { api, AppConfig } from '../lib/api';\nimport { useConfig } from '../context/ConfigContext';\nimport { toast } from 'sonner';\nimport { useLoggedIn } from '../context/LoginContext';\nimport { TtsProvider, availableProviders, findVoice } from '../lib/voices';\nimport { VoicePicker } from '../components/VoicePicker';\n\ntype LogType = 'danmu' | 'gift' | 'interact' | 'other' | 'system';\n\ninterface LogEntry {\n  id: number;\n  type: LogType;\n  text: string;\n  time: string;\n  user?: string;\n  content?: string;\n}\n\nlet _logId = 0;\n\nfunction parseMonitorLog(text: string): LogEntry | null {\n  if (!text) return null;\n  const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();\n  const id = _logId++;\n\n  if (text.startsWith('弹幕 ')) {\n    const content = text.slice(3);\n    const splitIdx = content.indexOf(': ');\n    if (splitIdx !== -1) {\n      const user = content.slice(0, splitIdx);\n      const msg = content.slice(splitIdx + 2);\n      return { id, type: 'danmu', text, user, content: msg, time };\n    }\n  }\n  if (text.startsWith('礼物 ')) return { id, type: 'gift', text, time };\n  if (text.startsWith('进入 ') || text.startsWith('关注 ') || text.startsWith('分享 ')) {\n    return { id, type: 'interact', text, time };\n  }\n  if (text.startsWith('禁言 ') || text.startsWith('PK ') || text.startsWith('红包 ') || text.startsWith('天选 ')) {\n    return { id, type: 'other', text, time };\n  }\n  if (text.startsWith('人气 ')) return null;\n  return { id, type: 'system', text, time };\n}\n\nconst typeColors: Record<LogType, string> = {\n  danmu: 'text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200',\n  gift: 'text-amber-500 font-bold',\n  interact: 'text-blue-500',\n  other: 'text-purple-500',\n  system: 'text-gray-400 italic',\n};\n\nconst typeBadge: Record<LogType, string> = {\n  danmu: '弹幕',\n  gift: '礼物',\n  interact: '互动',\n  other: '其他',\n  system: '系统',\n};\n\nexport function Monitor() {\n  const { config, updateConfigImmediate } = useConfig();\n  const [filter, setFilter] = useState('all');\n  const [message, setMessage] = useState('');\n  const [isMonitoring, setIsMonitoring] = useState(false);\n  const [showLogs, setShowLogs] = useState(true); \n  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<LogEntry[]>([]);\n  \n  const [voiceOpen, setVoiceOpen] = useState(false);\n\n  const logEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n  const bufferRef = useRef<LogEntry[]>([]);\n  const loggedIn = useLoggedIn();\n\n  // 关键：实时刷新逻辑\n  const flushLogs = useCallback(() => {\n    if (!showLogs || bufferRef.current.length === 0) return;\n    const itemsToFlush = [...bufferRef.current];\n    bufferRef.current = [];\n    setLogs(prev => {\n      const next = [...prev, ...itemsToFlush];\n      return next.length > 500 ? next.slice(next.length - 500) : next;\n    });\n  }, [showLogs]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    // 初始加载历史\n    api.getMonitorStatus().then(setIsMonitoring).catch(console.error);\n    api.getMonitorLogs().then(rawLogs => {\n      const history = (rawLogs || []).map(parseMonitorLog).filter((e): e is LogEntry => e !== null).slice(-100);\n      bufferRef.current = [...history];\n      flushLogs();\n    }).catch(console.error);\n\n    // 轮询 + 事件监听双保险\n    const pollTimer = setInterval(async () => {\n      if (!showLogs || !isMonitoring) return;\n      try {\n        const lines = await api.getRecentDanmaku();\n        if (lines && lines.length > 0) {\n          lines.forEach(line => {\n            const entry = parseMonitorLog(line);\n            if (entry) bufferRef.current.push(entry);\n          });\n        }\n      } catch (err) { console.error('[Monitor] Poll failed', err); }\n    }, 500);\n\n    const flushTimer = setInterval(() => { if (showLogs && bufferRef.current.length > 0) flushLogs(); }, 600);\n\n    let unlLog: any, unlStatus: any;\n    api.onMonitorLog(text => {\n      if (!showLogs) return;\n      const entry = parseMonitorLog(text);\n      if (entry) { bufferRef.current.push(entry); flushLogs(); }\n    }).then(fn => unlLog = fn);\n\n    api.onMonitorStatus(s => setIsMonitoring(s === '运行中')).then(fn => unlStatus = fn);\n\n    return () => {\n      clearInterval(pollTimer); clearInterval(flushTimer);\n      unlLog?.(); unlStatus?.();\n    };\n  }, [showLogs, isMonitoring, flushLogs]);\n\n  useEffect(() => { logEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' }); }, [logs]);\n\n  const toggleMonitorShow = () => {\n    if (!loggedIn) { toast.info('请先登录'); return; }\n    setShowLogs(!showLogs);\n    toast.success(!showLogs ? '已恢复读取弹幕' : '已暂停界面显示');\n  };\n\n  const handleStartConnection = async () => {\n    try {\n      await api.startMonitor();\n      setIsMonitoring(true);\n      toast.success('正在尝试建立直播间连接...');\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(`连接请求发送失败: ${err}`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleTtsToggle = async (val: boolean) => {\n    if (!config) return;\n    const next = { ...config, TtsEnabled: val };\n    updateConfigImmediate(next);\n    await api.saveConfig(next);\n    toast.success(val ? '已开启弹幕播报' : '已关闭弹幕播报');\n  };\n\n  const sendDanmu = async () => {\n    if (!loggedIn) { toast.info('请先登录'); return; }\n    if (!message.trim()) return;\n    try { await api.sendDanmu(message); setMessage(''); } \n    catch (err) { toast.error(`发送失败: ${err}`); }\n  };\n\n  const ttsProviders = useMemo(() => (config?.AiProviders ?? []).filter(p => p.ProviderType === 'tts' && p.Enabled && (p.Name.includes('Edge') || !!p.APIKey)), [config]);\n  \n  // 自动选择第一个可用的 TTS 引擎\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (config && !config.ActiveTtsProviderId && ttsProviders.length > 0) {\n      const next = { ...config, ActiveTtsProviderId: ttsProviders[0].Id };\n      updateConfigImmediate(next);\n      api.saveConfig(next);\n    }\n  }, [config, ttsProviders]);\n\n  const filteredLogsList = useMemo(() => logs.filter(log => log.type !== 'system' && (filter === 'all' || log.type === filter)), [logs, filter]);\n\n  if (!config) return null;\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"p-4 h-full flex flex-col gap-4 overflow-hidden\">\n      <GlassCard className=\"flex-1 p-4 flex flex-col overflow-hidden\">\n        <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between mb-3 shrink-0\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3\">\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5\">\n              <div className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${isMonitoring && showLogs ? 'bg-green-500 animate-pulse' : 'bg-gray-400'}`} />\n              <span className=\"text-[12px] font-bold text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200\">\n                {isMonitoring ? (showLogs ? '同步' : '暂停') : '未连接'}\n              </span>\n            </div>\n            <button onClick={toggleMonitorShow} className={`h-7 px-3 rounded-lg text-[11px] font-bold border ${showLogs ? 'bg-orange-500/10 text-orange-600 border-orange-500/20' : 'bg-blue-500/10 text-blue-600 border-blue-500/20'}`}>{showLogs ? '暂停读取' : '开始读取'}</button>\n            <div className=\"w-px h-4 bg-gray-200\" />\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n              <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 rounded-lg bg-black/5 border border-gray-200\">\n                <Volume2 className={`w-3.5 h-3.5 ${config.TtsEnabled ? 'text-[var(--primary-color)]' : 'text-gray-400'}`} />\n                <span className=\"text-[11px] font-medium text-gray-500\">读取弹幕</span>\n                <Toggle checked={!!config.TtsEnabled} onChange={handleTtsToggle} />\n              </div>\n              {config.TtsEnabled && (\n                <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5 animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-left-2 duration-300\">\n                  <select value={config.ActiveTtsProviderId || ''} onChange={e => { const next = {...config, ActiveTtsProviderId: e.target.value}; updateConfigImmediate(next); api.saveConfig(next); }} \n                          disabled={ttsProviders.length === 0}\n                          className=\"h-7 px-1.5 rounded-lg bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 text-[10px] focus:outline-none\">\n                    {ttsProviders.length === 0 && <option value=\"\">未配置 TTS</option>}\n                    {ttsProviders.map(p => <option key={p.Id} value={p.Id}>{p.Name}</option>)}\n                  </select>\n                  <button onClick={() => setVoiceOpen(true)} className=\"flex items-center gap-1 h-7 px-2 rounded-lg bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 text-[10px] text-gray-600\">\n                    <span className=\"max-w-[70px] truncate font-medium\">{(() => { const v = (['edge_tts','minimax_tts','volcano_engine'] as any[]).reduce<any>((found, p) => found ?? findVoice(p, config.TtsVoice), undefined); return v ? v.name : '声音'; })()}</span>\n                    <ChevronDown className=\"w-3 h-3 opacity-50\" />\n                  </button>\n                </div>\n              )}\n            </div>\n            <VoicePicker open={voiceOpen} onClose={() => setVoiceOpen(false)} providers={availableProviders(ttsProviders.map(p => p.Name))} currentVoice={config.TtsVoice || ''} onSelect={async v => { const next = {...config, TtsVoice: v}; updateConfigImmediate(next); await api.saveConfig(next); }} />\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex gap-1.5\">\n            {['all', 'danmaku', 'gift', 'interact', 'other'].map(id => (<button key={id} onClick={() => setFilter(id)} className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-[11px] transition-all ${filter === id ? 'bg-[var(--primary-color)] text-white' : 'bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 hover:bg-white'}`}>{typeBadge[id as LogType] || '全部'}</button>))}\n            <button onClick={() => setLogs([])} className=\"px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-[11px] bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 hover:bg-white ml-2\">清空记录</button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto space-y-0.5 bg-black/5 dark:bg-black/20 p-3 rounded-lg\">\n          {filteredLogsList.map(log => (\n            <div key={log.id} className=\"flex items-start gap-2 py-1 border-b border-black/5 dark:border-white/5 text-[11px]\">\n              <span className=\"text-gray-400 shrink-0 font-mono w-[52px]\">{log.time}</span>\n              <span className={`shrink-0 font-semibold w-[28px] ${typeColors[log.type]}`}>{typeBadge[log.type]}</span>\n              <span className=\"break-all\">{log.type === 'danmu' ? <><span className=\"font-medium\">{log.user}</span><span className=\"text-gray-400 mx-1\">:</span><span>{log.content}</span></> : <span>{log.text}</span>}</span>\n            </div>\n          ))}\n          <div ref={logEndRef} />\n          {filteredLogsList.length === 0 && (<div className=\"text-gray-400 text-center py-10 italic text-[11px]\">{!isMonitoring ? []).filter(p => p.ProviderType === 'tts' && p.Enabled && (p.Name.includes('Edge') || !!p.APIKey)), [config]);\n  \n  // 自动选择第一个可用的 TTS 引擎\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (config && !config.ActiveTtsProviderId && ttsProviders.length > 0) {\n      const next = { ...config, ActiveTtsProviderId: ttsProviders[0].Id };\n      updateConfigImmediate(next);\n      api.saveConfig(next);\n    }\n  }, [config, ttsProviders]);\n\n  const filteredLogsList = useMemo(() => logs.filter(log => log.type !== 'system' && (filter === 'all' || log.type === filter)), [logs, filter]);\n\n  if (!config) return null;\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"p-4 h-full flex flex-col gap-4 overflow-hidden\">\n      <GlassCard className=\"flex-1 p-4 flex flex-col overflow-hidden\">\n        <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between mb-3 shrink-0\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3\">\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5\">\n              <div className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${isMonitoring && showLogs ? 'bg-green-500 animate-pulse' : 'bg-gray-400'}`} />\n              <span className=\"text-[12px] font-bold text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200\">\n                {isMonitoring ? (showLogs ? '同步' : '暂停') : '未连接'}\n              </span>\n            </div>\n            <button onClick={toggleMonitorShow} className={`h-7 px-3 rounded-lg text-[11px] font-bold border ${showLogs ? 'bg-orange-500/10 text-orange-600 border-orange-500/20' : 'bg-blue-500/10 text-blue-600 border-blue-500/20'}`}>{showLogs ? '暂停读取' : '开始读取'}</button>\n            <div className=\"w-px h-4 bg-gray-200\" />\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n              <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 rounded-lg bg-black/5 border border-gray-200\">\n                <Volume2 className={`w-3.5 h-3.5 ${config.TtsEnabled ? 'text-[var(--primary-color)]' : 'text-gray-400'}`} />\n                <span className=\"text-[11px] font-medium text-gray-500\">读取弹幕</span>\n                <Toggle checked={!!config.TtsEnabled} onChange={handleTtsToggle} />\n              </div>\n              {config.TtsEnabled && (\n                <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5 animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-left-2 duration-300\">\n                  <select value={config.ActiveTtsProviderId || ''} onChange={e => { const next = {...config, ActiveTtsProviderId: e.target.value}; updateConfigImmediate(next); api.saveConfig(next); }} \n                          disabled={ttsProviders.length === 0}\n                          className=\"h-7 px-1.5 rounded-lg bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 text-[10px] focus:outline-none\">\n                    {ttsProviders.length === 0 && <option value=\"\">未配置 TTS</option>}\n                    {ttsProviders.map(p => <option key={p.Id} value={p.Id}>{p.Name}</option>)}\n                  </select>\n                  <button onClick={() => setVoiceOpen(true)} className=\"flex items-center gap-1 h-7 px-2 rounded-lg bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 text-[10px] text-gray-600\">\n                    <span className=\"max-w-[70px] truncate font-medium\">{(() => { const v = (['edge_tts','minimax_tts','volcano_engine'] as any[]).reduce<any>((found, p) => found ?? findVoice(p, config.TtsVoice), undefined); return v ? v.name : '声音'; })()}</span>\n                    <ChevronDown className=\"w-3 h-3 opacity-50\" />\n                  </button>\n                </div>\n              )}\n            </div>\n            <VoicePicker open={voiceOpen} onClose={() => setVoiceOpen(false)} providers={availableProviders(ttsProviders.map(p => p.Name))} currentVoice={config.TtsVoice || ''} onSelect={async v => { const next = {...config, TtsVoice: v}; updateConfigImmediate(next); await api.saveConfig(next); }} />\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex gap-1.5\">\n            {['all', 'danmaku', 'gift', 'interact', 'other'].map(id => (<button key={id} onClick={() => setFilter(id)} className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-[11px] transition-all ${filter === id ? 'bg-[var(--primary-color)] text-white' : 'bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 hover:bg-white'}`}>{typeBadge[id as LogType] || '全部'}</button>))}\n            <button onClick={() => setLogs([])} className=\"px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-[11px] bg-white/60 border border-gray-200 hover:bg-white ml-2\">清空记录</button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto space-y-0.5 bg-black/5 dark:bg-black/20 p-3 rounded-lg\">\n          {filteredLogsList.map(log => (\n            <div key={log.id} className=\"flex items-start gap-2 py-1 border-b border-black/5 dark:border-white/5 text-[11px]\">\n              <span className=\"text-gray-400 shrink-0 font-mono w-[52px]\">{log.time}</span>\n              <span className={`shrink-0 font-semibold w-[28px] ${typeColors[log.type]}`}>{typeBadge[log.type]}</span>\n              <span className=\"break-all\">{log.type === 'danmu' ? <><span className=\"font-medium\">{log.user}</span><span className=\"text-gray-400 mx-1\">:</span><span>{log.content}</span></> : <span>{log.text}</span>}</span>\n            </div>\n          ))}\n          <div ref={logEndRef} />\n          {filteredLogsList.length === 0 && (<div className=\"text-gray-400 text-center py-10 italic text-[11px]\">{!isMonitoring ? '请先在右下角建立连接' : !showLogs ? '已暂停读取，记录已隐藏' : '等待记录中...'}</div>)}\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      <GlassCard className=\"p-4 shrink-0\">\n        <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n          <Input value={message} onChange={e => setMessage(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && sendDanmu()} placeholder=\"输入要发送的弹幕…\" className=\"flex-1 h-10 text-[12px] px-4 rounded-xl\" maxLength={30} />\n          <Button variant=\"primary\" onClick={sendDanmu} disabled={!loggedIn || !message.trim()} className=\"min-w-[80px]\">发送弹幕</Button>\n          {!isMonitoring && (<button onClick={handleStartConnection} title=\"建立连接\" className=\"w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center bg-[var(--primary-color)] text-white shadow-lg active:scale-95 transition-all\"><RefreshCw className=\"w-5 h-5\" /></button>)}\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 mt-2 text-right\">{message.length}/30</div>\n      </GlassCard>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

        <div className=\"p-3 rounded-xl bg-white/40 border border-gray-200 space-y-1.5\">\n            <label className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400\">盲盒频率(s)</label>\n            <Input          <div className=\"p-3 rounded-xl bg-white/40 border border-gray-200 flex items-center justify-between\">\n            <span className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400\">@ 用户</span>\n            <Toggle checked={!!config.ThanksGiftUseAt} onChange={() => toggle('ThanksGiftUseAt')} />\n          </div>\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"space-y-2\">\n          <label {'{value}'}</p>\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"space-y-3 pt-4 border-t border-gray-200/50\">\n          <label className=\"text-[11px] font-bold text-gray-500 flex items-center onClick={() => { const next = { ...(config.GiftAliases || {}) }; delete next[k]; save({ ...config, GiftAliases: next }); }}><X className=\"w-2.5 h-2.5\" /></button></span>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    ),\n    interact: (\n      <div className=\"space-y-6\">\n        <section className=\"space-y-3\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center </div>\n          <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n            <Input value={newFocusMsg} onChange={e => setNewFocusMsg(e.target.value)} placeholder=\"添加关注台词...\" className=\"flex-1 h-9 text-[12px]\" </div>\n                <Input value={blackUidInput} onChange={e => /^\\d*$/.test(e.target.value) && setBlackUidInput(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && (()=>{ const v = parseInt(blackUidInput); if(!isNaN(v)) save({...config, PermanentBlacklistUsers:[...(config.PermanentBlacklistUsers || []), v]}); setBlackUidInput(''); })()} placeholder=\"UID 回车...\" className=\"h-8 text-[11px] border-none bg-white\" />\n             </div>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"space-y-2\">\n             <label className=\"text-[11px] font-bold text-gray-400 text-[13px] bg-white/60\" />\n          </GlassCard>\n          <GlassCard className=\"p-5 border-orange-500/20 bg-orange-500/5 space-y-4\">\n             <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3\">\n ## MODEL ✨

I have restored all the UI and configuration improvements as requested. I have reversed the previous rollback and re-applied the following features:

### 1. Global UI & Notifications
- **Toast Notifications:** Restored to the **top-right** (above the avatar area), with `fit-content` sizing and a smooth **1.5s fade-out** animation.
- **Sidebar Navigation:**
    - Renamed **"房间管理"** back to **"弹幕管理" (Danmaku Management)**.
    - Reorganized the menu to place **"数据统计" (Data Statistics)** immediately under the Dashboard.

### 2. AI Robot & TTS Configuration
- **Advanced TTS Filtering:** The dropdowns in both the **AI Robot** and **Danmaku Management** pages now only show providers that are both **Enabled** and **Configured** (e.g., cloud services must have a saved API Key).
- **Auto-Selection:** If no TTS engine is selected, the application will automatically pick the first functional one from your list.
- **UI Refinements:** Restored the polished dropdown menus and placeholders ("未配置 TTS" when empty).

### 3. Settings Panel Improvements
- **Simplified Paths:** Labels updated to **"配置文件位置"**, now showing only the **filename** for a cleaner look.
- **Folder Access:** Restored the **folder icon** next to file paths, allowing you to open the directory directly in your system file explorer.
- **Cleaned Actions:** Removed the redundant copy path button as requested.

### 4. Modernized Backend (Preserved)
- **TOML Configuration:** The transition from YAML to TOML is complete and stable (`etc/bilidanmaku-api.toml`).
- **Data Cleanup:** The automatic task that removes database records **older than 30 days** every 24 hours remains active.
- **Streamlined logic:** Removed the obsolete "New User Welcome" feature from both the frontend and backend engine.

The application is now back in its modernized state with all your preferred refinements active and verified. Please let me know if you need anything else!

    "output": "import { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect, useCallback, ReactNode } from 'react';\nimport { api, AppConfig } from '../lib/api';\nimport { toast } from 'sonner';\n\ninterface ConfigContextType {\n  config: AppConfig | null;\n  loading: boolean;\n  refreshConfig: () => Promise<void>;\n  updateConfig: (patch: Partial<AppConfig>) => Promise<void>;\n  updateConfigImmediate: (patch: Partial<AppConfig>) => void;\n}\n\nconst ConfigContext = createContext<ConfigContextType | undefined>(undefined);\n\nexport function ConfigProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {\n  const [config, setConfig] = useState<AppConfig | null>(null);\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);\n\n  const refreshConfig = useCallback(async () => {\n    try {\n      const cfg = await api.loadConfig();\n      setConfig(cfg);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to load config:', err);\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false);\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  const updateConfig = useCallback(async (patch: Partial<AppConfig>) => {\n    if (!config) return;\n    const next = { ...config, ...patch };\n    // 乐观更新 UI\n    setConfig(next);\n    try {\n      await api.saveConfig(next);\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(`保存配置失败: ${err}`);\n      // 回滚\n      refreshConfig();\n      throw err;\n    }\n  }, [config, refreshConfig]);\n\n  const updateConfigImmediate = useCallback((patch: Partial<AppConfig>) => {\n    setConfig(prev => prev ? { ...prev, ...patch } : null);\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    refreshConfig();\n  }, [refreshConfig]);\n\n  return (\n    <ConfigContext.Provider value={{ config, loading, refreshConfig, updateConfig, updateConfigImmediate }}>\n      {children}\n    </ConfigContext.Provider>\n  );\n}\n\nexport function useConfig() {\n  const context = useContext(ConfigContext);\n  if (context === undefined) {\n    throw new Error('useConfig must be used within a ConfigProvider');\n  }\n  return context;\n}\n"
  }
}

AutoGroup[] = [\n  {\n    title: 'AI 机器人', Icon: Bot, mainKey: 'AiReplyToDanmaku', to: '/ai',\n    subs: [\n      { label: '关注答谢',   key: 'ThanksFocus' },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    title: '自动欢迎', Icon: ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\nexport function Dashboard() {\n  const navigate = useNavigate();\n  const { config, updateConfig } = useConfig();\n  const {});\n    \n    const interval = setInterval(async () => {\n      try {\n        const m = await api.getMonitorStatus();\n        setIsMonitoring(m);\n        if (m) {\n          const s = await value: boolean) => {\n    await updateConfig({ [key]: value });\n  };\n\n  const statItems = useMemo(() => [\n    { label: '本场弹幕', value: stats?.danmu_count  || 0, icon: MessageSquare },\n    { label:
